<a id="28157" href="Frame.html#28092" class="Function">frame-is-univ-str</a> <a id="28175" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28177" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#2442" class="Function">SNS‚ÜíUnivalentStr</a> <a id="28194" href="Frame.html#25563" class="Function">isHomoEqv</a> <a id="28204" href="Frame.html#27650" class="Function">frame-is-SNS</a>

<a id="28218" class="Comment">-- Similar to the poset case, this is sufficient to establish that the category of frames</a>
<a id="28308" class="Comment">-- is univalent</a>

<a id="‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°"></a><a id="28325" href="Frame.html#28325" class="Function">‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°</a> <a id="28330" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28332" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28333" href="Frame.html#28333" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="28335" href="Frame.html#28335" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="28337" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28339" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="28345" href="Basis.html#2598" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="28348" href="Basis.html#2601" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="28351" href="Basis.html#2604" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÇ</a><a id="28353" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28355" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="28357" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28358" href="Frame.html#28333" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="28360" href="Frame.html#25803" class="Function Operator">‚âÉf</a> <a id="28363" href="Frame.html#28335" class="Bound">G</a><a id="28364" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28366" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Glue.html#1051" class="Function Operator">‚âÉ</a> <a id="28368" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28369" href="Frame.html#28333" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="28371" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="28373" href="Frame.html#28335" class="Bound">G</a><a id="28374" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="28376" href="Frame.html#28325" class="Function">‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°</a> <a id="28381" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28383" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#4416" class="Function">SIP</a> <a id="28387" href="Frame.html#28092" class="Function">frame-is-univ-str</a>

<a id="28406" class="Comment">-- However, there are two minor issues with this.</a>
<a id="28456" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="28459" class="Comment">--   1. We do not have to talk about equivalences as we are talking about sets;</a>
<a id="28539" class="Comment">--      isomorphisms are well-behaved in our case as we are dealing with sets.</a>
<a id="28618" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="28621" class="Comment">--  2. We do not have to require the frame data to be preserved. We can show that any</a>
<a id="28707" class="Comment">--     poset isomorphism preserves the frame operators.</a>
<a id="28763" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="28766" class="Comment">-- We will therefore strengthen our result to work with the notion of poset isomorphism.</a>

<a id="28856" class="Comment">-- We start by showing the equivalence between ‚âÉf and ‚âÖ‚Çö.</a>

<a id="34357" class="Comment">-- Now that we have this result, we can move on to show that given two frames F and G,</a>
<a id="34444" class="Comment">-- (pos F) ‚âÖ‚Çö (pos G) is equivalent to F ‚â° G.</a>
